			function setAutoCompleteTermCount() {
				var t = polaris.search.form.find("#keyword").val();
				if (polaris.autoComplete && polaris.autoComplete.terms && polaris.autoComplete.terms.length) {
					for (x = 0; x < polaris.autoComplete.terms.length; x++) {
						if (t ==  polaris.autoComplete.terms[x].term) {
							polaris.search.form.find("#termCount").val(polaris.autoComplete.terms[x].count);
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
		
			function unbindAndSubmitForm() {
				polaris.search.form.unbind("submit");
				polaris.search.form.submit();
				return false;
			}
			
			function loadGoogleMap(){
				if (polaris.geoCoder === null){

					script.type = "text/javascript";
					script.src = "http://maps.googleapis.com/maps/api/js?sensor=false&callback=geocodeCallback";
					document.body.appendChild(script);
				} else if (typeof geoinit === 'function') {
					geoinit();
				}
			}
		
			polaris.search.form.bind("submit",function(evt) {

			function setAutoCompleteTermCount() {
				var t = polaris.search.form.find("#keyword").val();
				if (polaris.autoComplete && polaris.autoComplete.terms && polaris.autoComplete.terms.length) {
					for (x = 0; x < polaris.autoComplete.terms.length; x++) {
						if (t ==  polaris.autoComplete.terms[x].term) {
							polaris.search.form.find("#termCount").val(polaris.autoComplete.terms[x].count);
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
		
			function unbindAndSubmitForm() {
				polaris.search.form.unbind("submit");
				polaris.search.form.submit();
				return false;
			}
			
			function loadGoogleMap(){
				if (polaris.geoCoder === null){
					var script = document.createElement("script");
					script.type = "text/javascript";
					script.src = "http://maps.googleapis.com/maps/api/js?sensor=false&callback=geocodeCallback";
					document.body.appendChild(script);
				} else if (typeof geoinit === 'function') {
					geoinit();
				}
			}
		
			polaris.search.form.bind("submit",function(evt) {
				loadGoogleMap();
				setAutoCompleteTermCount();
				return polaris.search.geocoded(disableSubmitButton, unbindAndSubmitForm);
			});

			function setAutoCompleteTermCount() {
				var t = polaris.search.form.find("#keyword").val();
				if (polaris.autoComplete && polaris.autoComplete.terms && polaris.autoComplete.terms.length) {
					for (x = 0; x < polaris.autoComplete.terms.length; x++) {

							polaris.search.form.find("#termCount").val(polaris.autoComplete.terms[x].count);
						}
					}
				}
			}

			function setAutoCompleteTermCount() {
				var t = polaris.search.form.find("#keyword").val();
				if (polaris.autoComplete && polaris.autoComplete.terms && polaris.autoComplete.terms.length) {
					for (x = 0; x < polaris.autoComplete.terms.length; x++) {
						if (t ==  polaris.autoComplete.terms[x].term) {
							polaris.search.form.find("#termCount").val(polaris.autoComplete.terms[x].count);
						}
					}
				}
			}

					document.body.appendChild(script);
				} else if (typeof geoinit === 'function') {
					geoinit();
				}
			}

			function setAutoCompleteTermCount() {
				var t = polaris.search.form.find("#keyword").val();
				if (polaris.autoComplete && polaris.autoComplete.terms && polaris.autoComplete.terms.length) {
					for (x = 0; x < polaris.autoComplete.terms.length; x++) {
						if (t ==  polaris.autoComplete.terms[x].term) {
							polaris.search.form.find("#termCount").val(polaris.autoComplete.terms[x].count);
						}
					}
				}
			}

					document.body.appendChild(script);
				} else if (typeof geoinit === 'function') {
					geoinit();
				}
			}

			function setAutoCompleteTermCount() {
				var t = polaris.search.form.find("#keyword").val();
				if (polaris.autoComplete && polaris.autoComplete.terms && polaris.autoComplete.terms.length) {
					for (x = 0; x < polaris.autoComplete.terms.length; x++) {
						if (t ==  polaris.autoComplete.terms[x].term) {
							polaris.search.form.find("#termCount").val(polaris.autoComplete.terms[x].count);
						}
					}
				}
			}

					document.body.appendChild(script);
				} else if (typeof geoinit === 'function') {
					geoinit();
				}
			}

		$('#list-view-toggle').click(function() {
			$.cookielet('')
		});
		
		// Apply qtip to active element 
		if(isGalleryView) {
			$('#list-view-toggle').qtip({
				content: {
					text: "Switch to list view"
				},
				position: {
					my: 'bottom left',
					at: 'top right'
				}
			});
		}
		else {
			$('#gallery-view-toggle').qtip({
				content: {
					text: "Switch to gallery view"
				},
				position: {
					my: 'bottom left',
					at: 'top right'
				}
			});	
		}
		
		// Sets the correct selected value for the sort

		// Generate dropdown
		$("#search-sort-select").msDropDown({rowHeight: 27 });
		
		// Navigate to the new sort URL when selected from list
		$('#search-sort-select').change(function() {
			window.location.href = $(this).val();
		});
		
		// Adds function to auto update on a select change
		$('.ec-attribute .ec-select').change(function() {
			$(this).parents('form:first').submit();
		});
		
		// Sets the default selected value for radius
		$('#radius').val('');

						props = {
							'total_search_results': 89

						if (elemType) {
							mixpanel.register({'AdSense clicked' : true});							
							props['adsense_position']=elemType;

						}

						return props;
					}
